divClass, delay){\nthis.content=content //message array content\nthis.tickerid=divId //ID of ticker div to display information\nthis.delay=delay //Delay between msg change, in width of inner DIVs to outer DIV's width minus padding (padding assumed to be top padding x 2)\nthis.visiblediv.style.width=this.hiddendiv.style.width=this.tickerdiv.offsetWidth-(this.visibledivtop*2)+\"px\"\nthis.getinline(this.visiblediv, (window.attachEvent) //Clean up loose references in IE\nwindow.attachEvent(\"onunload\", function(){scrollerinstance.tickerdiv.onmouseover=scrollerinstance.tickerdiv.onmouseout=null})\nsetTimeout(function(){scrollerinstance.animateup()}, this.delay)\n}\n\n\n// div2){\ndiv1.style.top=this.visibledivtop+\"px\"\ndiv2.style.top=Math.max(div1.parentNode.offsetHeight, div1.offsetHeight)+\"px\"\n}\n\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n// setmessage()- Populate the hidden div with the next message before it's visible\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n\npausescroller.prototype.setmessage=function(){\nvar scrollerinstance=this\nif (this.mouseoverBol==1) //if mouse is currently over up-down scroller- © Dynamic Drive (www.dynamicdrive.com)\n* This notice MUST stay intact for legal use\n* Visit http://www.dynamicdrive.com/ for this script and 100s more.\n***********************************************/\n\nfunction pausescroller(content, divId, divClass, delay){\nthis.content=content //message array content\nthis.tickerid=divId //ID of ticker div to display information\nthis.delay=delay //Delay between msg change, in miliseconds.\nthis.mouseoverBol=0 //Boolean to indicate whether mouse is currently over scroller (and pause it if it is)\nthis.hiddendivpointer=1 //index of message array for hidden div\ndocument.write('<div id=\"'+divId+'\" class=\"'+divClass+'\" style=\"position: relative; overflow: hidden\"><div style=\"position: absolute; width: 100%\" id=\"'+divId+'1\">'+content[0]+'</div><div style=\"position: absolute; width: 100%; visibility: hidden\" id=\"'+divId+'2\">'+content[1]+'</div></div>')\nvar scrollerinstance=this\nif (window.addEventListener) //run onload in DOM2 browsers\nwindow.addEventListener(\"load\", function(){scrollerinstance.initialize()}, false)\nelse if (window.attachEvent) //run onload in IE5.5+\nwindow.attachEvent(\"onload\", function(){scrollerinstance.initialize()})\nelse if (document.getElementById) //if legacy DOM browsers, just start scroller after 0.5 sec\nsetTimeout(function(){scrollerinstance.initialize()}, 500)\n}\n\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n// initialize()- Initialize scroller method.\n// -Get div objects, set initial positions, start up down animation\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n\npausescroller.prototype.initialize=function(){\nthis.tickerdiv=document.getElementById(this.tickerid)\nthis.visiblediv=document.getElementById(this.tickerid+\"1\")\nthis.hiddendiv=document.getElementById(this.tickerid+\"2\")\nthis.visibledivtop=parseInt(pausescroller.getCSSpadding(this.tickerdiv))\n//set width of inner DIVs to outer DIV's width minus padding (padding assumed to be top padding x 2)\nthis.visiblediv.style.width=this.hiddendiv.style.width=this.tickerdiv.offsetWidth-(this.visibledivtop*2)+\"px\"\nthis.getinline(this.visiblediv, this.hiddendiv)\nthis.hiddendiv.style.visibility=\"visible\"\nvar scrollerinstance=this\ndocument.getElementById(this.tickerid).onmouseover=function(){scrollerinstance.mouseoverBol=1}\ndocument.getElementById(this.tickerid).onmouseout=function(){scrollerinstance.mouseoverBol=0}\nif (window.attachEvent) //Clean up loose references in IE\nwindow.attachEvent(\"onunload\", function(){scrollerinstance.tickerdiv.onmouseover=scrollerinstance.tickerdiv.onmouseout=null})\nsetTimeout(function(){scrollerinstance.animateup()}, this.delay)\n}\n\n\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n// animateup()- Move the two inner divs of the scroller up and in sync\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n\npausescroller.prototype.animateup=function(){\nvar scrollerinstance=this\nif (parseInt(this.hiddendiv.style.top)>(this.visibledivtop+5)){\nthis.visiblediv.style.top=parseInt(this.visiblediv.style.top)-5+\"px\"\nthis.hiddendiv.style.top=parseInt(this.hiddendiv.style.top)-5+\"px\"\nsetTimeout(function(){scrollerinstance.animateup()}, 50)\n}\nelse{\nthis.getinline(this.hiddendiv, this.visiblediv)\nthis.swapdivs()\nsetTimeout(function(){scrollerinstance.setmessage()}, this.delay)\n}\n}\n\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n// swapdivs()- Swap between which is the visible and which is the hidden div\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n\npausescroller.prototype.swapdivs=function(){\nvar tempcontainer=this.visiblediv\nthis.visiblediv=this.hiddendiv\nthis.hiddendiv=tempcontainer\n}\n\npausescroller.prototype.getinline=function(div1, div2){\ndiv1.style.top=this.visibledivtop+\"px\"\ndiv2.style.top=Math.max(div1.parentNode.offsetHeight, div1.offsetHeight)+\"px\"\n}\n\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n// setmessage()- Populate the hidden div with the next message before it's visible\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------\n\npausescroller.prototype.setmessage=function(){\nvar scrollerinstance=this\nif (this.mouseoverBol==1) //if mouse is currently over scoller, do nothing (pause it)\nsetTimeout(function(){scrollerinstance.setmessage()}, 500)\nelse{\nvar i=this.hiddendivpointer\nvar ceiling=this.content.length\nthis.hiddendivpointer=(i+1>ceiling-1)? 0 : i+1\nthis.hiddendiv.innerHTML=this.content[this.hiddendivpointer]\nthis.animateup()\n}\n}\n\npausescroller.getCSSpadding=function(tickerobj){ //get CSS padding value, if any\nif (tickerobj.currentStyle)\nreturn tickerobj.currentStyle[\"paddingTop\"]\nelse if (window.getComputedStyle) //if DOM2\nreturn window.getComputedStyle(tickerobj, \"\").getPropertyValue(\"padding-top\")\nelse\nreturn 0\n}\n\n</script>\n\n\n<script type=\"text/javascript\">\n\n//new pausescroller(name_of_message_array, CSS_ID, CSS_classname,
